Non-linear warp of QSM Map/Maps to MNI space using the FSL MNI152 1 mm Template:

MNI outputs will be placed in /home/data3/vzachari/QSM_Toolkit/QSM_Test_Run/S1090/QSM/FreeSurf_QSM_Masks/MNI152_QSM

This script is useful for:

1) Voxelwise QSM analyses
2) For aligning your own MNI ROIs and/or masks on the QSM Maps

Example code for aligning a mask in MNI space to the QSM Maps.

		#Your mask in MNI space needs to be in S1090/QSM/FreeSurf_QSM_Masks/MNI152_QSM
		singularity run -e --bind /home/data3/vzachari/QSM_Toolkit/QSM_Test_Run/S1090/QSM/FreeSurf_QSM_Masks/MNI152_QSM \ 
			/home/data3/vzachari/QSM_Toolkit/IronSmithQSM/Functions/QSM_Container.simg 		\ 
			3dNwarpApply -source YOUR_MASK_IN_MNI_GOES_HERE.nii.gz					\ 
			  -master S1090_freesurfer_brain_AL_Mag_MNI152+tlrc					\ 
			  -ainterp NN -iwarp -nwarp anat.un.aff.qw_WARP.nii anat.un.aff.Xat.1D			\ 
			  -prefix NAME_FOR_YOUR_MASK_IN_NATIVE_SPACE_GOES_HERE.nii.gz 		          	  

---------------------------------------------------------------
